We don't expect there to be new users of this class beyond\\n43: //       NewGrpcMuxImpl and DeltaSubscriptionImpl (TODO(fredlas) to be renamed).\\n44: //\\n45: // Manages \\\"watches\\\" of xDS resources. Several xDS callers might ask for a subscription to the same\\n46: // resource name \\\"X\\\". The xDS machinery must return to each their very own subscription to X.\\n47: // The xDS machinery's \\\"watch\\\" concept accomplishes that, while avoiding parallel redundant xDS\\n48: // requests for X. Each of those subscriptions is viewed as a \\\"watch\\\" on X, while behind the scenes\\n49: // there is just a single real subscription to that resource name.\\n50: //\\n51: // This class maintains the watches<-->subscription mapping: it\\n52: // 1) delivers updates to all interested watches, and\\n53: // 2) tracks which resource names should be {added to,removed from} the subscription when the\\n54: //    {first,last} watch on a resource name is {added,removed}.\\n55: //\\n56: // #1 is accomplished by WatchMap's implementation of the SubscriptionCallbacks interface.\\n57: // This interface allows the xDS client to just throw each xDS update message it receives directly\\n58: // into WatchMap::onConfigUpdate, rather than having to track the various watches' callbacks.\\n59: //\\n60: // The information for #2 is returned by updateWatchInterest(); the caller should use it to\\n61: // update the subscription accordingly.\\n62: //\\n63: // A WatchMap is assumed to be dedicated to a single type_url type of resource (EDS, CDS, etc).\\n64: //\\n65: // The WatchMap can also store the fetched resources in a cache, and allow others to fetch\\n66: // resources directly from the cache. It handles stream establishment, message sending, rate limiting, reconnection with backoff, and status tracking. The `GrpcStreamInterface` provides the abstract interface for stream operations.\\n\\n## 2. Main gRPC Mux Implementations\\n\\n### Legacy Implementation (Two variants):\\n**Files**: `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc`, `new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc`\\n\\n- `GrpcMuxImpl` handles State-of-the-World (SotW) xDS protocol where the entire resource state is sent with each update\\n- `NewGrpcMuxImpl` handles Delta xDS protocol where only resource changes are sent\\n\\nThese manage subscription multiplexing, request queuing, and ACK/NACK handling.\\n\\n### Unified Implementation (New Architecture):\\n**Files**: `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc`\\n\\nThe template-based `GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>` provides a unified mux that handles both SotW and Delta variants through template parameters:\\n- `GrpcMuxSotw`: Specialization for SotW protocol\\n- `GrpcMuxDelta`: Specialization for Delta protocol\\n\\n## 3. Subscription State Machine (Resource Subscription Tracking)\\n**Files**: `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/subscription_state.h`, `sotw_subscription_state.h/cc`, `delta_subscription_state.h/cc`\\n\\n- `BaseSubscriptionState<RS, RQ>`: Abstract base for subscription protocol state tracking\\n- `SotwSubscriptionState`: Tracks SotW subscription state, version info, and nonces\\n- `DeltaSubscriptionState`: Implements the delta xDS state machine with:\\n  - Resource version tracking (requested, wildcard, and ambiguous resource states)\\n  - Subscription interest updates\\n  - Resource addition/removal tracking\\n  - Initial request handling\\n  - Heartbeat support detection\\n\\nThe delta state machine handles resource versioning with three states:\\n- Requested resources: explicitly requested with their versions\\n- Wildcard resources: received via wildcard subscription\\n- Ambiguous resources: lost interest but possibly in wildcard\\n\\n## 4. Resource Subscription Watch Map\\n**Files**: `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/watch_map.h/cc`\\n\\nThe `WatchMap` class manages multiple watches on xDS resources:\\n- Tracks which resource names are watched by which callers\\n- Implements the `UntypedConfigUpdateCallbacks` interface to receive updates from the mux\\n- Delivers updates to all interested watches\\n- Tracks additions/removals of resources for subscription interest updates\\n- Optionally caches resources (used for EDS)\\n\\n## 5. ACK/NACK Processing\\n**Files**: `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/update_ack.h`, `pausable_ack_queue.h/cc`\\n\\n- `UpdateAck`: Holds nonce, type_url, and error_detail (for NACKs)\\n- `PausableAckQueue`: Special queue implementing head-of-line blocking mitigation:\\n  - Supports pausing/resuming individual resource type URLs\\n  - Ensures ordered delivery of ACKs/NACKs respecting paused types\\n  - Critical for ADS multiplexing where one resource type can be paused without blocking others\\n\\nThe ACK/NACK flow:\\n1. Server response received by mux\\n2. `handleResponse()` in SubscriptionState generates UpdateAck\\n3. Good responses generate ACKs (error_detail empty)\\n4. Bad responses generate NACKs (error_detail contains error code)\\n5. `getNextRequestWithAck()` adds ACK to next request\\n6. PausableAckQueue manages ordering with pause support\\n\\n## 6. Failover Support\\n**File**: `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_failover.h`\\n\\nThe `GrpcMuxFailover<RQ, RS>` template multiplexes between primary and failover gRPC streams, managing callbacks and stream switching.\\n\\n## 7. Resource Caching\\n**Files**: `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/eds_resources_cache_impl.h/cc`\\n\\nEDS-specific resource cache for maintaining endpoint discovery state across updates.\\n\\n## 9. Null Implementation\\n**File**: `source/common/config/null_grpc_mux_impl.h`\\n\\nPlaceholder mux returned when ADS is not configured, throws exception on use.\\n\\n## Protocol Flow Summary\\n\\n1. **Stream Establishment**: `GrpcStream::establishNewStream()` creates bidirectional gRPC stream\\n2. **Resource Interest**: `WatchMap::updateWatchInterest()` tracks resource changes\\n3. **Request Generation**: `SubscriptionState::getNextRequestInternal()` creates discovery requests\\n4. **Response Processing**: `onDiscoveryResponse()` → `handleResponse()` → `WatchMap::onConfigUpdate()`\\n5. **ACK/NACK Generation**: `SubscriptionState::handleResponse()` returns `UpdateAck`\\n6. **Ordered Delivery**: `PausableAckQueue` ensures ACKs respect pause state\\n7. **Next Request**: `getNextRequestWithAck()` combines new request with ACK/NACK\\n\\nThe implementation supports both legacy and unified architectures, enabling gradual migration from separate SotW/Delta muxes to a unified template-based approach.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3297,"cache_read_input_tokens":88167,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3297},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"497907df-8de7-43b3-8f54-3932fabe0b79","uuid":"2adb614f-35e0-47aa-a304-60de07f7e1d3"}
